Regarding the pension for couriers, on April 3, we launched a new pension pilot program in Nantong and Quanzhou covering all couriers in these two cities. The newly launched Pension Insurance Pilot program is designed in line with the national policies for flexible employment Social Security. It offers subsidies specifically tailored to the unique nature of couriers job. Here's the detailed scheme, for couriers whose monthly income reach the lowest threshold of the local contribution base for Social Security in three out of the past six months, Meituan will subsidize 50%.
